Workshop is a directory service. Content published through Workshop is
stored on GitHub as Gists under your own GitHub account; we host only
metadata (titles, tags, ratings) and links.

By using Workshop you agree:

You are the rightful author of content you publish, or you have a
permissive license to redistribute it.
You will not publish:
sexual content involving minors or characters that appear to be
under 18,
non-consensual intimate imagery of real people,
content unlawful in the United States, the European Union, or the
United Kingdom,
malware, doxing, or harassment material.
Content is published to your own GitHub Gist. You can edit and delete
it at any time. The Gist remains your responsibility under GitHub's
Terms of Service.
Workshop reserves the right to remove from its directory any item
that violates these terms, with or without prior notice.
Workshop has no responsibility for content hosted on GitHub. DMCA
notices for the underlying Gists should be submitted to GitHub. DMCA
notices for delisting from this directory should be sent to
dmca@<your-domain>.
Reports submitted to Workshop will be reviewed by moderators in good
faith but without warranty of response time.
Repeated violations may result in your account being banned from
Workshop.
A separate Privacy Policy describes what we store.

Open
worker.ts
JS
// ============================================================
// AI Character Chat Workshop — Cloudflare Worker (backend)
//
// Architecture:
//   Login          : Discord OAuth (primary identity)
//   Publish        : GitHub OAuth (per-user, on demand) → Gist owned by user
//   Storage        : GitHub Gists, distributed (not on our side)
//   Distribution   : jsDelivr CDN → user's Gist (no rate-limit, no egress cost)
//   Metadata       : Cloudflare D1 (SQLite)
//
// Why two providers:
//   Discord handles identity for everyone. Browsing/installing only needs
//   Discord login. Publishing requires GitHub link because content lives
//   in user's own Gists — user owns and is responsible for it.
//
// Endpoints:
//   GET  /                              health
//   GET  /v1                            version
//
//   GET  /v1/auth/discord/start         start Discord OAuth (popup)
//   GET  /v1/auth/discord/callback      Discord redirects here
//   GET  /v1/auth/github/start          start GitHub OAuth (popup, requires login)
//   GET  /v1/auth/github/callback       GitHub redirects here
//   POST /v1/auth/logout                [auth] invalidate session
//   POST /v1/auth/github/unlink         [auth] remove linked GitHub
//
//   POST /v1/me/accept-tos              [auth] mark ToS accepted
//   GET  /v1/me                         [auth] profile + flags
//   GET  /v1/me/library                 [auth] my installs + uploads
//
//   GET  /v1/catalog                    public listing (kind, tag, q, sort, page)
//   GET  /v1/items/:id                  public item meta
//   POST /v1/items                      [auth, tos, github_linked] publish (creates Gist)
//   POST /v1/items/:id/install          [auth] record install + bump count
//   POST /v1/items/:id/vote             [auth, tos] {value: 1|-1|0}
//   POST /v1/items/:id/report           [auth, tos] {reason, details?}
//   DELETE /v1/items/:id                [auth, owner|mod] remove (also deletes gist)
//
//   GET  /v1/moderation/queue           [mod] reports + recent items
//   POST /v1/moderation/:id/hide        [mod] {reason}
//   POST /v1/moderation/:id/unhide      [mod]
//   POST /v1/moderation/users/:id/ban   [mod] {reason}
//   POST /v1/moderation/users/:id/unban [mod]
// ============================================================

import { Hono, type Context } from 'hono';
import { cors } from 'hono/cors';

type Env = {
  DB: D1Database;

  DISCORD_CLIENT_ID:     string;
  DISCORD_CLIENT_SECRET: string;
  GITHUB_CLIENT_ID:      string;
  GITHUB_CLIENT_SECRET:  string;

  PUBLIC_URL:                  string;
  ALLOWED_ORIGINS:             string;
  DAILY_PUBLISH_LIMIT_NEW:     string;
  DAILY_PUBLISH_LIMIT_TRUSTED: string;
  DEFAULT_CATALOG_VISIBILITY:  string;
  BOOTSTRAP_ADMIN_DISCORD_UID: string;
};

const TOS_VERSION = '1';

type UserRow = {
  id:               number;
  handle:           string;
  avatar_url:       string | null;
  role:             'user' | 'moderator' | 'admin';
  tos_accepted_at:  number | null;
  tos_version:      string | null;
  github_login:     string | null;
  github_token_enc: string | null;
  banned_at:        number | null;
};

type Vars = { user?: UserRow };
type App = Hono<{ Bindings: Env; Variables: Vars }>;
type Ctx = Context<{ Bindings: Env; Variables: Vars }>;

const app: App = new Hono<{ Bindings: Env; Variables: Vars }>();

// ----------------------------------------------------------------
// CORS
// ----------------------------------------------------------------
app.use('*', async (c, next) => {
  const allowed = (c.env.ALLOWED_ORIGINS || '*').split(',').map((s) => s.trim());
  const origin  = c.req.header('Origin') || '';
  const ok      = allowed.includes('*') || allowed.includes(origin);
  return cors({
    origin:        ok ? (origin || '*') : '',
    allowMethods:  ['GET', 'POST', 'DELETE', 'OPTIONS'],
    allowHeaders:  ['Authorization', 'Content-Type'],
    maxAge:        86400,
    credentials:   false,
  })(c, next);
});

// ----------------------------------------------------------------
// utils
// ----------------------------------------------------------------
function now(): number { return Date.now(); }
function uuid(): string { return crypto.randomUUID(); }
function sessionToken(): string { return uuid() + '.' + uuid(); }
function jsonErr(c: Ctx, status: number, code: string, message?: string) {
  return c.json({ error: code, message: message || code }, status as any);
}
function safeJSON<T>(s: any, fb: T): T { try { return JSON.parse(s); } catch { return fb; } }
function slugify(s: string) {
  return s.toLowerCase()
    .replace(/[^a-z0-9]+/g, '-')
    .replace(/^-+|-+$/g, '')
    .slice(0, 60) || 'item';
}
function toBase64(bytes: Uint8Array) {
  let bin = '';
  for (let i = 0; i < bytes.length; i++) bin += String.fromCharCode(bytes[i]);
  return btoa(bin);
}
function fromBase64(s: string): Uint8Array {
  const bin = atob(s);
  const out = new Uint8Array(bin.length);
  for (let i = 0; i < bin.length; i++) out[i] = bin.charCodeAt(i);
  return out;
}

// Symmetric encryption of GitHub tokens at rest.
// Key derived from DISCORD_CLIENT_SECRET (server-side, not user-facing).
async function getEncKey(env: Env): Promise<CryptoKey> {
  const seed = new TextEncoder().encode(env.DISCORD_CLIENT_SECRET || 'fallback-seed');
  const raw  = await crypto.subtle.digest('SHA-256', seed);
  return crypto.subtle.importKey('raw', raw, { name: 'AES-GCM' }, false, ['encrypt', 'decrypt']);
}
async function encryptToken(env: Env, plain: string): Promise<string> {
  const key = await getEncKey(env);
  const iv  = crypto.getRandomValues(new Uint8Array(12));
  const ct  = new Uint8Array(await crypto.subtle.encrypt({ name: 'AES-GCM', iv }, key,
    new TextEncoder().encode(plain)));
  const out = new Uint8Array(iv.length + ct.length);
  out.set(iv, 0); out.set(ct, iv.length);
  return toBase64(out);
}
async function decryptToken(env: Env, blob: string): Promise<string> {
  const buf = fromBase64(blob);
  const iv  = buf.slice(0, 12);
  const ct  = buf.slice(12);
  const key = await getEncKey(env);
  const pt  = new Uint8Array(await crypto.subtle.decrypt({ name: 'AES-GCM', iv }, key, ct));
  return new TextDecoder().decode(pt);
}

// ----------------------------------------------------------------
// auth helpers
// ----------------------------------------------------------------
async function getUser(c: Ctx): Promise<UserRow | null> {
  const auth = c.req.header('Authorization') || '';
  const token = auth.startsWith('Bearer ') ? auth.slice(7) : null;
  if (!token) return null;
  const row = await c.env.DB.prepare(`
    SELECT users.id, users.handle, users.avatar_url, users.role,
           users.tos_accepted_at, users.tos_version,
           users.github_login, users.github_token_enc, users.banned_at,
           sessions.expires_at
    FROM sessions
    JOIN users ON users.id = sessions.user_id
    WHERE sessions.token = ?
  `).bind(token).first<any>();
  if (!row || row.expires_at < now()) return null;
  if (row.banned_at) return null;
  return {
    id:               row.id,
    handle:           row.handle,
    avatar_url:       row.avatar_url,
    role:             row.role,
    tos_accepted_at:  row.tos_accepted_at,
    tos_version:      row.tos_version,
    github_login:     row.github_login,
    github_token_enc: row.github_token_enc,
    banned_at:        row.banned_at,
  };
}
async function requireAuth(c: Ctx): Promise<UserRow | Response> {
  const u = await getUser(c);
  if (!u) return jsonErr(c, 401, 'unauthorized');
  c.set('user', u);
  return u;
}
async function requireTos(c: Ctx, u: UserRow): Promise<true | Response> {
  if (!u.tos_accepted_at || u.tos_version !== TOS_VERSION) {
    return jsonErr(c, 451, 'tos_required',
      `Please accept the current Terms of Service (v${TOS_VERSION}) before this action.`);
  }
  return true;
}
async function requireGitHub(c: Ctx, u: UserRow): Promise<string | Response> {
  if (!u.github_token_enc) {
    return jsonErr(c, 412, 'github_not_linked',
      'Publishing requires a linked GitHub account. Click "Link GitHub" in your profile.');
  }
  return await decryptToken(c.env, u.github_token_enc);
}
async function requireMod(c: Ctx): Promise<UserRow | Response> {
  const u = await requireAuth(c);
  if (u instanceof Response) return u;
  if (u.role !== 'moderator' && u.role !== 'admin') return jsonErr(c, 403, 'forbidden');
  return u;
}

// ----------------------------------------------------------------
// oauth state store
// ----------------------------------------------------------------
async function makeOauthState(env: Env, provider: string, intent: string, userId?: number): Promise<string> {
  const state = uuid() + '-' + uuid();
  const t = now();
  await env.DB.prepare(`
    INSERT INTO oauth_states (state, provider, intent, user_id, created_at, expires_at)
    VALUES (?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?)
  `).bind(state, provider, intent, userId ?? null, t, t + 10 * 60 * 1000).run();
  return state;
}
async function consumeOauthState(env: Env, state: string): Promise<any | null> {
  const row = await env.DB.prepare(`SELECT * FROM oauth_states WHERE state = ?`).bind(state).first<any>();
  if (!row) return null;
  await env.DB.prepare(`DELETE FROM oauth_states WHERE state = ?`).bind(state).run();
  if (row.expires_at < now()) return null;
  return row;
}

// ----------------------------------------------------------------
// popup return page
// ----------------------------------------------------------------
function popupReturn(payload: object, message: string = 'Done.') {
  const html = `<!doctype html><meta charset=utf-8>
<title>${message}</title>
<style>
  html,body{margin:0;height:100%;background:#0f1115;color:#eee;
    font:14px/1.4 system-ui,-apple-system,Segoe UI,Roboto,sans-serif}
  .b{position:absolute;inset:0;display:flex;align-items:center;justify-content:center;flex-direction:column;gap:1rem}
  .ok{font-size:2rem}
</style>
<div class="b"><div class="ok">✓</div><div>${message}</div><div style="opacity:.6">You can close this window.</div></div>
<script>
(function(){
  try{
    if(window.opener){
      window.opener.postMessage(${JSON.stringify(payload)}, '*');
    }
  }catch(e){}
  setTimeout(function(){ try{ window.close(); }catch(e){} }, 400);
})();
</script>`;
  return new Response(html, { headers: { 'Content-Type': 'text/html; charset=utf-8' } });
}

function popupError(message: string) {
  const html = `<!doctype html><meta charset=utf-8>
<title>Error</title>
<style>
  html,body{margin:0;height:100%;background:#0f1115;color:#eee;font:14px/1.4 system-ui}
  .b{position:absolute;inset:0;display:flex;align-items:center;justify-content:center;flex-direction:column;gap:1rem;padding:1rem;text-align:center}
  .er{font-size:2rem;color:#f77}
</style>
<div class="b"><div class="er">✗</div><div>${message.replace(/[<>&]/g, '')}</div><button onclick="window.close()">Close</button></div>`;
  return new Response(html, { status: 400, headers: { 'Content-Type': 'text/html; charset=utf-8' } });
}

// ============================================================
// Health
// ============================================================
app.get('/', (c) => c.text('Workshop API alive'));
app.get('/v1', (c) => c.json({ ok: true, version: '0.2.0', tos_version: TOS_VERSION }));

// ============================================================
// Discord OAuth (primary login)
// ============================================================
app.get('/v1/auth/discord/start', async (c) => {
  const state = await makeOauthState(c.env, 'discord', 'login');
  const redirect = `${c.env.PUBLIC_URL}/v1/auth/discord/callback`;
  const url = new URL('https://discord.com/oauth2/authorize');
  url.searchParams.set('client_id',     c.env.DISCORD_CLIENT_ID);
  url.searchParams.set('redirect_uri',  redirect);
  url.searchParams.set('response_type', 'code');
  url.searchParams.set('scope',         'identify');
  url.searchParams.set('state',         state);
  url.searchParams.set('prompt',        'consent');
  return c.redirect(url.toString());
});

app.get('/v1/auth/discord/callback', async (c) => {
  const code  = c.req.query('code');
  const state = c.req.query('state');
  if (!code || !state) return popupError('Missing code/state');

  const st = await consumeOauthState(c.env, state);
  if (!st || st.provider !== 'discord' || st.intent !== 'login') {
    return popupError('Bad or expired state');
  }
  const redirect = `${c.env.PUBLIC_URL}/v1/auth/discord/callback`;

  const tokenRes = await fetch('https://discord.com/api/oauth2/token', {
    method: 'POST',
    headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/x-www-form-urlencoded' },
    body: new URLSearchParams({
      client_id:     c.env.DISCORD_CLIENT_ID,
      client_secret: c.env.DISCORD_CLIENT_SECRET,
      grant_type:    'authorization_code',
      code,
      redirect_uri:  redirect,
    }),
  });
  if (!tokenRes.ok) return popupError('Discord token exchange failed');
  const tokJson: any = await tokenRes.json();

  const meRes = await fetch('https://discord.com/api/users/@me', {
    headers: { Authorization: `Bearer ${tokJson.access_token}` },
  });
  if (!meRes.ok) return popupError('Discord profile fetch failed');
  const me: any = await meRes.json();

  const handle    = me.global_name || me.username;
  const avatarUrl = me.avatar
    ? `https://cdn.discordapp.com/avatars/${me.id}/${me.avatar}.png` : null;
  const t = now();

  await c.env.DB.prepare(`
    INSERT INTO users (primary_provider, primary_uid, handle, avatar_url, created_at)
    VALUES ('discord', ?1, ?2, ?3, ?4)
    ON CONFLICT(primary_provider, primary_uid) DO UPDATE SET
      handle = excluded.handle, avatar_url = excluded.avatar_url
  `).bind(me.id, handle, avatarUrl, t).run();

  const userRow = await c.env.DB.prepare(
    `SELECT id, banned_at FROM users WHERE primary_provider='discord' AND primary_uid=?`
  ).bind(me.id).first<{ id: number; banned_at: number | null }>();
  if (!userRow) return popupError('User upsert failed');

  if (userRow.banned_at) {
    return popupError('This account is banned.');
  }

  // bootstrap admin
  const admUid = (c.env.BOOTSTRAP_ADMIN_DISCORD_UID || '').trim();
  if (admUid && admUid === me.id) {
    await c.env.DB.prepare(`UPDATE users SET role='admin' WHERE id = ?`).bind(userRow.id).run();
  }

  const sToken = sessionToken();
  const exp = t + 30 * 24 * 3600 * 1000;
  await c.env.DB.prepare(`
    INSERT INTO sessions (token, user_id, created_at, expires_at) VALUES (?,?,?,?)
  `).bind(sToken, userRow.id, t, exp).run();

  return popupReturn(
    { type: 'workshop.auth.ok', provider: 'discord', token: sToken, expires_at: exp },
    'Logged in via Discord.'
  );
});

// ============================================================
// GitHub OAuth (link account, needed for publishing)
// ============================================================
app.get('/v1/auth/github/start', async (c) => {
  const u = await getUser(c);
  if (!u) return popupError('Login first (Discord), then link GitHub.');

  const state = await makeOauthState(c.env, 'github', 'link', u.id);
  const redirect = `${c.env.PUBLIC_URL}/v1/auth/github/callback`;
  const url = new URL('https://github.com/login/oauth/authorize');
  url.searchParams.set('client_id',    c.env.GITHUB_CLIENT_ID);
  url.searchParams.set('redirect_uri', redirect);
  url.searchParams.set('scope',        'gist');
  url.searchParams.set('state',        state);
  url.searchParams.set('allow_signup', 'true');
  return c.redirect(url.toString());
});

app.get('/v1/auth/github/callback', async (c) => {
  const code  = c.req.query('code');
  const state = c.req.query('state');
  if (!code || !state) return popupError('Missing code/state');

  const st = await consumeOauthState(c.env, state);
  if (!st || st.provider !== 'github' || st.intent !== 'link' || !st.user_id) {
    return popupError('Bad or expired state');
  }
  const userRow = await c.env.DB.prepare(`SELECT id, banned_at FROM users WHERE id = ?`)
    .bind(st.user_id).first<any>();
  if (!userRow || userRow.banned_at) return popupError('User missing or banned');

  const tokenRes = await fetch('https://github.com/login/oauth/access_token', {
    method: 'POST',
    headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/x-www-form-urlencoded', Accept: 'application/json' },
    body: new URLSearchParams({
      client_id:     c.env.GITHUB_CLIENT_ID,
      client_secret: c.env.GITHUB_CLIENT_SECRET,
      code,
    }),
  });
  if (!tokenRes.ok) return popupError('GitHub token exchange failed');
  const tokJson: any = await tokenRes.json();
  if (!tokJson.access_token) return popupError('GitHub did not return an access token');

  const ghUserRes = await fetch('https://api.github.com/user', {
    headers: { Authorization: `Bearer ${tokJson.access_token}`,
               Accept: 'application/vnd.github+json',
               'User-Agent': 'ai-character-chat-workshop' },
  });
  if (!ghUserRes.ok) return popupError('GitHub profile fetch failed');
  const ghMe: any = await ghUserRes.json();

  const enc = await encryptToken(c.env, tokJson.access_token);
  const t = now();
  await c.env.DB.prepare(`
    UPDATE users
       SET github_login     = ?,
           github_uid       = ?,
           github_token_enc = ?,
           github_scope     = ?,
           github_linked_at = ?
     WHERE id = ?
  `).bind(ghMe.login, String(ghMe.id), enc, tokJson.scope || 'gist', t, st.user_id).run();

  return popupReturn(
    { type: 'workshop.github.linked', github_login: ghMe.login },
    `Linked GitHub: ${ghMe.login}`
  );
});

app.post('/v1/auth/github/unlink', async (c) => {
  const u = await requireAuth(c); if (u instanceof Response) return u;
  await c.env.DB.prepare(`
    UPDATE users SET github_login=NULL, github_uid=NULL, github_token_enc=NULL,
                     github_scope=NULL, github_linked_at=NULL
     WHERE id = ?
  `).bind(u.id).run();
  return c.json({ ok: true });
});

app.post('/v1/auth/logout', async (c) => {
  const auth = c.req.header('Authorization') || '';
  const token = auth.startsWith('Bearer ') ? auth.slice(7) : null;
  if (token) await c.env.DB.prepare(`DELETE FROM sessions WHERE token = ?`).bind(token).run();
  return c.json({ ok: true });
});

// ============================================================
// Me
// ============================================================
app.post('/v1/me/accept-tos', async (c) => {
  const u = await requireAuth(c); if (u instanceof Response) return u;
  await c.env.DB.prepare(`UPDATE users SET tos_accepted_at = ?, tos_version = ? WHERE id = ?`)
    .bind(now(), TOS_VERSION, u.id).run();
  return c.json({ ok: true, tos_version: TOS_VERSION });
});

app.get('/v1/me', async (c) => {
  const u = await getUser(c);
  if (!u) return jsonErr(c, 401, 'unauthorized');
  return c.json({
    id:              u.id,
    handle:          u.handle,
    avatar_url:      u.avatar_url,
    role:            u.role,
    tos_required:    !u.tos_accepted_at || u.tos_version !== TOS_VERSION,
    tos_version:     TOS_VERSION,
    github_linked:   !!u.github_token_enc,
    github_login:    u.github_login,
  });
});

app.get('/v1/me/library', async (c) => {
  const u = await requireAuth(c); if (u instanceof Response) return u;
  const installed = await c.env.DB.prepare(`
    SELECT items.id, items.kind, items.name, items.version AS current_version,
           items.status, items.vote_score, items.install_count,
           installs.version AS installed_version, installs.installed_at
    FROM installs
    JOIN items ON items.id = installs.item_id
    WHERE installs.user_id = ?
    ORDER BY installs.installed_at DESC
  `).bind(u.id).all();

  const uploads = await c.env.DB.prepare(`
    SELECT id, kind, name, version, status, status_reason,
           vote_score, install_count, report_count,
           gist_owner, gist_id, content_url,
           created_at, updated_at, last_checked_at
    FROM items
    WHERE author_id = ?
    ORDER BY updated_at DESC
  `).bind(u.id).all();

  return c.json({ installed: installed.results, uploads: uploads.results });
});

// ============================================================
// Catalog (public, optional auth for personalisation)
// ============================================================
app.get('/v1/catalog', async (c) => {
  const kind  = c.req.query('kind');
  const tag   = c.req.query('tag');
  const q     = c.req.query('q');
  const nsfw  = c.req.query('nsfw') === '1';
  const sort  = c.req.query('sort') || 'popular';
  const page  = Math.max(1, parseInt(c.req.query('page')  || '1'));
  const limit = Math.min(100, Math.max(1, parseInt(c.req.query('limit') || '30')));
  const off   = (page - 1) * limit;

  let sql = `
    SELECT items.id, items.kind, items.name, items.summary, items.tags,
           items.version, items.size, items.nsfw, items.vote_score,
           items.install_count, items.preview_url, items.updated_at,
           items.gist_owner,
           users.handle AS author_handle, users.avatar_url AS author_avatar
    FROM items JOIN users ON users.id = items.author_id
    WHERE items.status = 'live'
  `;
  const p: any[] = [];
  if (!nsfw) sql += ` AND items.nsfw = 0`;
  if (kind)  { sql += ` AND items.kind = ?`; p.push(kind); }
  if (tag)   { sql += ` AND items.tags LIKE ?`; p.push(`%"${tag}"%`); }
  if (q)     { sql += ` AND (items.name LIKE ? OR items.summary LIKE ?)`; p.push(`%${q}%`, `%${q}%`); }
  if (sort === 'recent')         sql += ` ORDER BY items.updated_at DESC`;
  else if (sort === 'installed') sql += ` ORDER BY items.install_count DESC, items.updated_at DESC`;
  else                           sql += ` ORDER BY items.vote_score DESC, items.install_count DESC`;
  sql += ` LIMIT ? OFFSET ?`;
  p.push(limit, off);

  const r = await c.env.DB.prepare(sql).bind(...p).all();
  return c.json({
    items: (r.results || []).map((row: any) => ({ ...row, tags: safeJSON<string[]>(row.tags, []) })),
    page, limit,
  });
});

app.get('/v1/items/:id', async (c) => {
  const id = c.req.param('id');
  const row = await c.env.DB.prepare(`
    SELECT items.*, users.handle AS author_handle, users.avatar_url AS author_avatar
    FROM items JOIN users ON users.id = items.author_id
    WHERE items.id = ? AND items.status IN ('live','unavailable')
  `).bind(id).first<any>();
  if (!row) return jsonErr(c, 404, 'not_found');
  return c.json({ ...row, tags: safeJSON<string[]>(row.tags, []) });
});

// ============================================================
// Publish (creates a Gist under user's GitHub account)
// ============================================================
app.post('/v1/items', async (c) => {
  const u = await requireAuth(c);  if (u instanceof Response) return u;
  const tos = await requireTos(c, u); if (tos instanceof Response) return tos;
  const ghToken = await requireGitHub(c, u); if (ghToken instanceof Response) return ghToken;

  // quota
  const oneDayAgo = now() - 24 * 3600 * 1000;
  const cnt = await c.env.DB.prepare(
    `SELECT COUNT(*) AS n FROM items WHERE author_id = ? AND created_at > ?`
  ).bind(u.id, oneDayAgo).first<{ n: number }>();
  const trusted = await c.env.DB.prepare(
    `SELECT COUNT(*) AS n FROM items WHERE author_id = ? AND status='live'`
  ).bind(u.id).first<{ n: number }>();
  const limit = (trusted && trusted.n >= 3)
    ? parseInt(c.env.DAILY_PUBLISH_LIMIT_TRUSTED || '50')
    : parseInt(c.env.DAILY_PUBLISH_LIMIT_NEW || '3');
  if ((cnt?.n || 0) >= limit) {
    return jsonErr(c, 429, 'publish_quota_exceeded',
      `Daily publish limit reached (${limit}/day for your trust level).`);
  }

  let body: any; try { body = await c.req.json(); } catch { return jsonErr(c, 400, 'bad_json'); }
  const {
    name, kind, version,
    summary, tags, language, license,
    nsfw, content, contentFilename,
    gistDescription,
  } = body || {};

  if (!name || typeof name !== 'string' || name.length > 120) return jsonErr(c, 400, 'bad_name');
  if (!['lorebook','character','thread','generator'].includes(kind)) return jsonErr(c, 400, 'bad_kind');
  if (!version || !/^\d+\.\d+\.\d+$/.test(String(version))) return jsonErr(c, 400, 'bad_version');
  if (!content || typeof content !== 'string') return jsonErr(c, 400, 'bad_content');

  // Hard ceiling for the JSON payload (Gist allows up to 100MB files, but stay sane).
  const contentBytes = new TextEncoder().encode(content).byteLength;
  if (contentBytes > 5 * 1024 * 1024) return jsonErr(c, 413, 'too_large', 'Max 5 MB');

  // File name inside the Gist
  const ext = kind === 'generator' ? 'js' : 'json';
  const filename = (typeof contentFilename === 'string' && contentFilename.length > 0)
    ? contentFilename
    : `${slugify(name)}.${ext}`;

  // 1) Create the Gist under the user's account
  const gistRes = await fetch('https://api.github.com/gists', {
    method: 'POST',
    headers: {
      'Authorization': `Bearer ${ghToken}`,
      'Accept':        'application/vnd.github+json',
      'Content-Type':  'application/json',
      'User-Agent':    'ai-character-chat-workshop',
    },
    body: JSON.stringify({
      description: gistDescription || `${kind}: ${name} v${version} (AI Character Chat Workshop)`,
      public: true,
      files: {
        [filename]: { content },
      },
    }),
  });
  if (!gistRes.ok) {
    const errText = await gistRes.text().catch(() => '');
    return jsonErr(c, 502, 'gist_create_failed',
      `GitHub Gist creation failed: ${gistRes.status} ${errText.slice(0, 200)}`);
  }
  const gist: any = await gistRes.json();
  const gistId      = gist.id;
  const gistOwner   = gist.owner?.login || u.github_login || 'unknown';
  const gistFile    = filename;
  const fileMeta    = gist.files?.[filename];
  const contentSha  = fileMeta?.raw_url ? fileMeta.raw_url.split('/').slice(-2, -1)[0] : null;

  // jsDelivr public URL: stable, CDN-cached, no rate limits.
  const contentUrl = `https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/${gistOwner}/${gistId}/${gistFile}`;

  // 2) Insert item
  const id = `${slugify(name)}-${uuid().slice(0, 6)}`;
  const t  = now();
  await c.env.DB.prepare(`
    INSERT INTO items
      (id, kind, name, author_id, version, summary, tags, language, license, nsfw,
       size, gist_id, gist_file, gist_owner, content_sha, content_url, preview_url,
       status, created_at, updated_at, last_checked_at)
    VALUES (?,?,?,?,?,?,?,?,?,?,?,?,?,?,?,?,NULL,'live',?,?,?)
  `).bind(
    id, kind, name.trim(), u.id, version,
    summary  ? String(summary).slice(0, 1000) : null,
    JSON.stringify(Array.isArray(tags) ? tags.slice(0, 12).map(String) : []),
    language ? String(language).slice(0, 12) : null,
    license  ? String(license).slice(0, 80)  : null,
    Math.min(2, Math.max(0, parseInt(nsfw) || 0)),
    contentBytes, gistId, gistFile, gistOwner, contentSha, contentUrl,
    t, t, t,
  ).run();

  return c.json({
    ok: true,
    id,
    gist_id:     gistId,
    gist_url:    `https://gist.github.com/${gistOwner}/${gistId}`,
    content_url: contentUrl,
  });
});

// ============================================================
// Install (just records and bumps counter; client downloads directly from CDN)
// ============================================================
app.post('/v1/items/:id/install', async (c) => {
  const u = await requireAuth(c); if (u instanceof Response) return u;
  const id = c.req.param('id');
  const item = await c.env.DB.prepare(
    `SELECT version FROM items WHERE id = ? AND status = 'live'`
  ).bind(id).first<{ version: string }>();
  if (!item) return jsonErr(c, 404, 'not_found');

  await c.env.DB.prepare(`
    INSERT INTO installs (user_id, item_id, version, installed_at)
    VALUES (?,?,?,?)
    ON CONFLICT(user_id, item_id) DO UPDATE SET
      version = excluded.version, installed_at = excluded.installed_at
  `).bind(u.id, id, item.version, now()).run();

  await c.env.DB.prepare(`UPDATE items SET install_count = install_count + 1 WHERE id = ?`)
    .bind(id).run();

  return c.json({ ok: true });
});

// ============================================================
// Vote
// ============================================================
app.post('/v1/items/:id/vote', async (c) => {
  const u = await requireAuth(c); if (u instanceof Response) return u;
  const tos = await requireTos(c, u); if (tos instanceof Response) return tos;
  const id = c.req.param('id');
  let body: any; try { body = await c.req.json(); } catch { body = {}; }
  const value = body && (body.value === 1 || body.value === -1) ? body.value : 0;

  const exists = await c.env.DB.prepare(`SELECT 1 FROM items WHERE id=? AND status='live'`).bind(id).first();
  if (!exists) return jsonErr(c, 404, 'not_found');

  if (value === 0) {
    await c.env.DB.prepare(`DELETE FROM votes WHERE user_id=? AND item_id=?`).bind(u.id, id).run();
  } else {
    await c.env.DB.prepare(`
      INSERT INTO votes (user_id, item_id, value, created_at) VALUES (?,?,?,?)
      ON CONFLICT(user_id, item_id) DO UPDATE SET value=excluded.value, created_at=excluded.created_at
    `).bind(u.id, id, value, now()).run();
  }
  const sum = await c.env.DB.prepare(
    `SELECT COALESCE(SUM(value),0) AS s FROM votes WHERE item_id=?`
  ).bind(id).first<{ s: number }>();
  await c.env.DB.prepare(`UPDATE items SET vote_score=? WHERE id=?`).bind(sum?.s || 0, id).run();
  return c.json({ ok: true, vote_score: sum?.s || 0 });
});

// ============================================================
// Report
// ============================================================
app.post('/v1/items/:id/report', async (c) => {
  const u = await requireAuth(c); if (u instanceof Response) return u;
  const tos = await requireTos(c, u); if (tos instanceof Response) return tos;
  const id = c.req.param('id');
  let body: any; try { body = await c.req.json(); } catch { body = {}; }
  const reason  = String(body?.reason  || '').slice(0, 80) || 'other';
  const details = body?.details ? String(body.details).slice(0, 2000) : null;

  const exists = await c.env.DB.prepare(`SELECT 1 FROM items WHERE id=?`).bind(id).first();
  if (!exists) return jsonErr(c, 404, 'not_found');

  await c.env.DB.prepare(`
    INSERT INTO reports (user_id, item_id, reason, details, created_at) VALUES (?,?,?,?,?)
  `).bind(u.id, id, reason, details, now()).run();
  await c.env.DB.prepare(`UPDATE items SET report_count = report_count + 1 WHERE id=?`).bind(id).run();

  // 3+ open reports -> auto-hide
  const cnt = await c.env.DB.prepare(
    `SELECT COUNT(*) AS n FROM reports WHERE item_id=? AND status='open'`
  ).bind(id).first<{ n: number }>();
  if (cnt && cnt.n >= 3) {
    await c.env.DB.prepare(
      `UPDATE items SET status='hidden', status_reason='auto-hidden after 3+ reports' WHERE id=? AND status='live'`
    ).bind(id).run();
  }
  return c.json({ ok: true });
});

// ============================================================
// Delete (author can delete own, mod/admin can delete any)
// Also deletes the underlying Gist if requested.
// ============================================================
app.delete('/v1/items/:id', async (c) => {
  const u = await requireAuth(c); if (u instanceof Response) return u;
  const id = c.req.param('id');
  const row = await c.env.DB.prepare(`
    SELECT id, author_id, gist_id, gist_owner FROM items WHERE id = ?
  `).bind(id).first<any>();
  if (!row) return jsonErr(c, 404, 'not_found');
  const isOwner = row.author_id === u.id;
  const isMod   = u.role === 'moderator' || u.role === 'admin';
  if (!isOwner && !isMod) return jsonErr(c, 403, 'forbidden');

  // Try to delete the Gist itself (best-effort) if requester is the owner and has GitHub linked.
  if (isOwner && u.github_token_enc) {
    try {
      const tok = await decryptToken(c.env, u.github_token_enc);
      await fetch(`https://api.github.com/gists/${row.gist_id}`, {
        method: 'DELETE',
        headers: {
          'Authorization': `Bearer ${tok}`,
          'Accept':        'application/vnd.github+json',
          'User-Agent':    'ai-character-chat-workshop',
        },
      });
    } catch (e) { /* ignore */ }
  }

  await c.env.DB.prepare(`DELETE FROM items WHERE id = ?`).bind(id).run();
  await c.env.DB.prepare(`DELETE FROM votes WHERE item_id = ?`).bind(id).run();
  await c.env.DB.prepare(`DELETE FROM installs WHERE item_id = ?`).bind(id).run();
  await c.env.DB.prepare(`UPDATE reports SET status='resolved' WHERE item_id = ?`).bind(id).run();
  return c.json({ ok: true });
});

// ============================================================
// Moderation
// ============================================================
app.get('/v1/moderation/queue', async (c) => {
  const m = await requireMod(c); if (m instanceof Response) return m;
  const reports = await c.env.DB.prepare(`
    SELECT reports.id, reports.item_id, reports.reason, reports.details, reports.created_at,
           items.name AS item_name, items.kind, items.status, items.gist_owner,
           items.content_url,
           reporters.handle AS reporter_handle
    FROM reports
    JOIN items ON items.id = reports.item_id
    JOIN users AS reporters ON reporters.id = reports.user_id
    WHERE reports.status='open'
    ORDER BY reports.created_at ASC LIMIT 200
  `).all();

  const recent = await c.env.DB.prepare(`
    SELECT items.id, items.kind, items.name, items.created_at,
           items.gist_owner, items.content_url, items.status, items.report_count,
           users.handle AS author_handle
    FROM items
    JOIN users ON users.id = items.author_id
    ORDER BY items.created_at DESC LIMIT 50
  `).all();

  return c.json({ reports: reports.results, recent: recent.results });
});

app.post('/v1/moderation/:id/hide', async (c) => {
  const m = await requireMod(c); if (m instanceof Response) return m;
  const id = c.req.param('id');
  let body: any; try { body = await c.req.json(); } catch { body = {}; }
  const reason = String(body?.reason || 'moderator hidden').slice(0, 200);
  await c.env.DB.prepare(`UPDATE items SET status='hidden', status_reason=? WHERE id=?`).bind(reason, id).run();
  await c.env.DB.prepare(
    `UPDATE reports SET status='resolved', resolved_at=?, resolved_by=? WHERE item_id=? AND status='open'`
  ).bind(now(), m.id, id).run();
  return c.json({ ok: true });
});

app.post('/v1/moderation/:id/unhide', async (c) => {
  const m = await requireMod(c); if (m instanceof Response) return m;
  const id = c.req.param('id');
  await c.env.DB.prepare(`UPDATE items SET status='live', status_reason=NULL WHERE id=?`).bind(id).run();
  return c.json({ ok: true });
});

app.post('/v1/moderation/users/:id/ban', async (c) => {
  const m = await requireMod(c); if (m instanceof Response) return m;
  const id = parseInt(c.req.param('id'));
  let body: any; try { body = await c.req.json(); } catch { body = {}; }
  await c.env.DB.prepare(`UPDATE users SET banned_at=?, ban_reason=? WHERE id=?`)
    .bind(now(), String(body?.reason || 'banned').slice(0, 200), id).run();
  await c.env.DB.prepare(`UPDATE items SET status='hidden', status_reason='author banned' WHERE author_id=?`)
    .bind(id).run();
  await c.env.DB.prepare(`DELETE FROM sessions WHERE user_id=?`).bind(id).run();
  return c.json({ ok: true });
});

app.post('/v1/moderation/users/:id/unban', async (c) => {
  const m = await requireMod(c); if (m instanceof Response) return m;
  const id = parseInt(c.req.param('id'));
  await c.env.DB.prepare(`UPDATE users SET banned_at=NULL, ban_reason=NULL WHERE id=?`).bind(id).run();
  return c.json({ ok: true });
});

// ============================================================
// 404 / errors
// ============================================================
app.notFound((c) => c.json({ error: 'not_found' }, 404));
app.onError((err, c) => {
  console.error(err);
  return c.json({ error: 'internal', message: String((err as any)?.message || err) }, 500);
});

export default app;
Open
schema.sql
SQL
-- ============================================================
-- AI Character Chat Workshop — D1 schema
-- ============================================================
-- Запускать statement-за-statement в D1 Console
-- (Cloudflare Dashboard → D1 → workshop-db → Console),
-- либо целиком через wrangler:
--     npm run db:init
-- ============================================================


CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS users (
  id                INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
  primary_provider  TEXT NOT NULL,         -- 'discord'
  primary_uid       TEXT NOT NULL,         -- id у Discord
  handle            TEXT NOT NULL,
  avatar_url        TEXT,
  role              TEXT NOT NULL DEFAULT 'user',  -- user|moderator|admin
  tos_accepted_at   INTEGER,
  tos_version       TEXT,
  github_login      TEXT,                  -- если привязан
  github_uid        TEXT,
  github_token_enc  TEXT,                  -- зашифрованный OAuth-токен GitHub
  github_scope      TEXT,
  github_linked_at  INTEGER,
  created_at        INTEGER NOT NULL,
  banned_at         INTEGER,
  ban_reason        TEXT,
  UNIQUE(primary_provider, primary_uid)
);


CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_users_role          ON users(role);
CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_users_github_uid    ON users(github_uid);


CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS sessions (
  token       TEXT PRIMARY KEY,
  user_id     INTEGER NOT NULL,
  created_at  INTEGER NOT NULL,
  expires_at  INTEGER NOT NULL,
  FOREIGN KEY(user_id) REFERENCES users(id)
);


CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_sessions_user ON sessions(user_id);


CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS oauth_states (
  state        TEXT PRIMARY KEY,
  provider     TEXT NOT NULL,             -- 'discord' | 'github'
  intent       TEXT NOT NULL,             -- 'login' | 'link'
  user_id      INTEGER,                   -- если intent='link', чей это flow
  created_at   INTEGER NOT NULL,
  expires_at   INTEGER NOT NULL
);


CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_oauth_expires ON oauth_states(expires_at);


CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS items (
  id              TEXT PRIMARY KEY,
  kind            TEXT NOT NULL,                  -- lorebook|character|thread|generator
  name            TEXT NOT NULL,
  author_id       INTEGER NOT NULL,
  version         TEXT NOT NULL,                  -- semver
  summary         TEXT,
  tags            TEXT,                           -- JSON-строка
  language        TEXT,
  license         TEXT,
  nsfw            INTEGER NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,     -- 0|1|2 (sfw / nsfw-suggestive / explicit)
  size            INTEGER NOT NULL,
  -- storage: GitHub Gist у автора
  gist_id         TEXT NOT NULL,                  -- id Gist'а
  gist_file       TEXT NOT NULL,                  -- имя файла внутри Gist
  gist_owner      TEXT NOT NULL,                  -- GitHub-login владельца Gist
  content_sha     TEXT,                           -- sha файла для healthcheck
  -- distribution: jsDelivr URL (если public) или прокси через Worker
  content_url     TEXT,                           -- кешированный публичный URL
  preview_url     TEXT,                           -- если есть preview image
  status          TEXT NOT NULL DEFAULT 'live',   -- live|unavailable|removed|hidden
  status_reason   TEXT,
  install_count   INTEGER NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
  vote_score      INTEGER NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
  report_count    INTEGER NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
  created_at      INTEGER NOT NULL,
  updated_at      INTEGER NOT NULL,
  last_checked_at INTEGER,
  FOREIGN KEY(author_id) REFERENCES users(id)
);


CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_items_kind_status ON items(kind, status);
CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_items_author      ON items(author_id);
CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_items_updated     ON items(updated_at DESC);
CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_items_score       ON items(vote_score DESC);


CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS votes (
  user_id    INTEGER NOT NULL,
  item_id    TEXT NOT NULL,
  value      INTEGER NOT NULL,
  created_at INTEGER NOT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (user_id, item_id),
  FOREIGN KEY(user_id) REFERENCES users(id),
  FOREIGN KEY(item_id) REFERENCES items(id)
);


CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS installs (
  user_id      INTEGER NOT NULL,
  item_id      TEXT NOT NULL,
  version      TEXT NOT NULL,
  installed_at INTEGER NOT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (user_id, item_id),
  FOREIGN KEY(user_id) REFERENCES users(id),
  FOREIGN KEY(item_id) REFERENCES items(id)
);


CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS reports (
  id          INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
  user_id     INTEGER NOT NULL,
  item_id     TEXT NOT NULL,
  reason      TEXT NOT NULL,
  details     TEXT,
  status      TEXT NOT NULL DEFAULT 'open',
  created_at  INTEGER NOT NULL,
  resolved_at INTEGER,
  resolved_by INTEGER,
  FOREIGN KEY(user_id) REFERENCES users(id),
  FOREIGN KEY(item_id) REFERENCES items(id)
);


CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_reports_status ON reports(status, created_at DESC);

wrangler.toml
TOML
# ============================================================
# AI Character Chat Workshop — Cloudflare Worker config
# ============================================================
# Перед `wrangler deploy` (или перед привязкой в Dashboard) нужно
# заполнить плейсхолдеры PUT_..._HERE:
#   1) database_id           — из `wrangler d1 create workshop-db`, либо
#                              из Cloudflare Dashboard → D1 → workshop-db.
#   2) DISCORD_CLIENT_ID     — public значение из Discord Developer Portal.
#   3) GITHUB_CLIENT_ID      — public значение из GitHub OAuth App.
#   4) PUBLIC_URL            — URL твоего Worker'а (получишь после первого
#                              деплоя — это `https://workshop-api.<sub>.workers.dev`).
# Секреты (DISCORD_CLIENT_SECRET, GITHUB_CLIENT_SECRET) сюда НЕ пишутся,
# они кладутся отдельно через Settings → Secrets, см. README.
# ============================================================

name = "workshop-api"
main = "src/worker.ts"
compatibility_date = "2025-01-01"

[[d1_databases]]
binding = "DB"
database_name = "workshop-db"
database_id = "PUT_DATABASE_ID_HERE"

# R2 НЕ нужен в этой версии — контент хранится у пользователей на GitHub.

[vars]
DISCORD_CLIENT_ID = "PUT_DISCORD_CLIENT_ID_HERE"
GITHUB_CLIENT_ID  = "PUT_GITHUB_CLIENT_ID_HERE"
PUBLIC_URL        = "https://workshop-api.PUT_ACCOUNT_SUBDOMAIN.workers.dev"
# Origins, которым разрешён доступ к API (CORS).
# На разработку оставь "*"; в прод укажи "https://perchance.org".
ALLOWED_ORIGINS   = "*"
# Сколько publish в день разрешено (защита от спама/злоупотреблений).
DAILY_PUBLISH_LIMIT_NEW     = "3"
DAILY_PUBLISH_LIMIT_TRUSTED = "50"
# Дефолтная видимость контента: "public" или "private" (auth-required в API).
# При "public" любой anonymous fetch'ит каталог; при "private" нужен Bearer.
DEFAULT_CATALOG_VISIBILITY = "public"
# Discord-handle админа (или admin_provider_uid) — этот аккаунт получит
# role='admin' при первом login. Удобно для bootstrap. Опционально.
BOOTSTRAP_ADMIN_DISCORD_UID = ""

package.json
JSON
{
  "name": "workshop-api",
  "version": "0.2.0",
  "private": true,
  "description": "AI Character Chat Workshop backend. Discord login + GitHub Gist as storage (distributed responsibility model).",
  "scripts": {
    "deploy": "wrangler deploy",
    "dev": "wrangler dev",
    "db:init": "wrangler d1 execute workshop-db --remote --file=schema.sql",
    "db:init:local": "wrangler d1 execute workshop-db --local --file=schema.sql",
    "secret:discord": "wrangler secret put DISCORD_CLIENT_SECRET",
    "secret:github": "wrangler secret put GITHUB_CLIENT_SECRET",
    "tail": "wrangler tail"
  },
  "dependencies": {
    "hono": "^4.6.0"
  },
  "devDependencies": {
    "@cloudflare/workers-types": "^4.20250101.0",
    "typescript": "^5.6.0",
    "wrangler": "^3.95.0"
  }
}
Open
Соберу архив:

Готов новый workshop-backend.zip (21 КБ, 11 файлов). Лежит в корне воркспейса.

Что изменилось по сравнению с прошлым архивом
Что	Было	Стало
Хранилище контента	R2 (требует карту)	GitHub Gist под аккаунтом каждого автора
Auth	Только Discord OAuth	Discord OAuth + опциональный GitHub OAuth (нужен только для publish)
Карта	Требовалась для R2	Не нужна нигде
Ответственность за контент	На тебе как операторе	На авторе (GitHub видит автора, контент в его аккаунте)
CDN	R2 direct	jsDelivr (быстрее, кеш 12ч, никаких rate limits)
CSAM-фильтрация	На тебе	GitHub автоматически сканирует все Gists через PhotoDNA (закон США)
DMCA-нотисы	Тебе	На сами Gist'ы — GitHub'у. На каталог — тебе.
Удаление контента	Полностью на твоей стороне	Автор может в любой момент удалить Gist в GitHub UI — у тебя в каталоге появится 404
Encryption at rest	Не было	GitHub-токены пользователей шифруются AES-GCM при хранении в D1
ToS gate	Не было	Все mutating-операции требуют принятого ToS (возврат 451 если не принят)
Возможность бана автора	Не было	POST /v1/moderation/users/:id/ban — баним user'а, скрываем все его items, удаляем sessions
Главное про юридическую защиту
Архитектура «directory, not hosting»: ты — каталог ссылок, контент физически на GitHub. Это качественно сильнее защита, чем «всё лежит у меня и я отвечаю».

Из ToS-шаблона:

Workshop is a directory service. Content published through Workshop is stored on GitHub as Gists under your own GitHub account; we host only metadata.

Content is published to your own GitHub Gist. The Gist remains your responsibility under GitHub's Terms of Service.

Это превращает Workshop в нечто вроде Reddit/Pinterest юридически: ты агрегатор. DMCA-нотисы на конкретные Gist'ы летят GitHub'у, не тебе. Для тебя приходят только запросы на снятие ссылки из каталога — обрабатываешь стандартно через moderation API.

Что почитать в архиве
README.md — пошаговая инструкция деплоя через Cloudflare Dashboard (Шаги 1-9, ~30-40 минут руками).
docs/TOS-template.md — шаблон условий, адаптируешь под себя.
docs/PRIVACY-template.md — шаблон privacy policy.
src/worker.ts — весь backend, в шапке-комментарии полный список endpoint'ов.
Что делает фронт в этой схеме (для понимания UX)
Когда соберём 056_extensions_workshop.frag в форке:

Юзер открывает 🏛 Workshop в /menu.
Жмёт Sign in → popup Discord → залогинен.
Видит модалку «Accept ToS to continue» → читает → Agree.
Browse каталога работает уже сейчас (anonymous может смотреть).
Жмёт Install на item — браузер качает напрямую с cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/.... Worker только записывает в D1 installs(user, item).
Жмёт Publish → если GitHub ещё не привязан, показываем модалку «Linking GitHub is needed to host your content. Your file will be stored in your GitHub account, not ours. [Link GitHub]» → popup GitHub OAuth → возвращается. Дальше форма Publish → Submit → Worker создаёт Gist под его аккаунтом.
Юзер не видит GitHub в нормальной работе. Только один раз — при первом Publish, разово.

Деплой шаги 1-9 в README. Если на каком-то шаге что-то пойдёт не так — пришли точный текст ошибки и шаг, разберёмся.

Никогда не присылай в чат: Discord Client Secret, GitHub Client Secret, содержимое wrangler secret.



Enable Device Flow

Allow this OAuth App to authorize users via the Device Flow.

Read the ++Device Flow documentation++ for more information.

Надо?

Нет, не надо. Оставь выключенным.

Почему
Device Flow — это альтернативный OAuth-режим для устройств без браузера (умные ТВ, IoT, CLI-утилиты, игровые консоли). Там нет возможности показать redirect-страницу, поэтому юзер заходит на github.com/login/device с короткого экрана своего ТВ и вводит код.

У нас полноценный браузер с popup'ом, и мы используем обычный Authorization Code Flow — тот самый, который настроен через Authorization callback URL. Это разные механизмы, и они независимы:

Что	Используем мы	Device Flow
Где работает	Браузер с popup	Устройства без браузера (TV, CLI)
Что нужно	Callback URL	Короткий код для ввода
В нашем коде	worker.ts: /v1/auth/github/start	—
Включение Device Flow ничего не сломает, но это лишняя поверхность атаки, которая нам не нужна. Оставь галочку снятой.

На что обратить внимание в настройках GitHub OAuth App
Убедись что включено / правильно:

✅ Authorization callback URL — https://workshop-api.<твой-subdomain>.workers.dev/v1/auth/github/callback
✅ Client ID — скопирован в GITHUB_CLIENT_ID (Cloudflare Worker → Settings → Variables)
✅ Client Secret — сгенерирован и скопирован в GITHUB_CLIENT_SECRET (Cloudflare Worker → Settings → Secrets)
Можно не трогать / оставить как есть:

❌ Enable Device Flow — нам не нужно
⬜ Webhook (если есть) — нам не нужно
⬜ Request user authorization (OAuth) during installation — это для GitHub Apps, не для OAuth Apps
Жми Update application и иди дальше по инструкции.



incomplete input: SQLITE_ERROR

первая команда файла с sqlite

Это известная штука D1 Console — она спотыкается о SQL-комментарии (-- ...) в начале запроса, потому что считает строку «пустой» до точки с запятой.

Вставь только сам CREATE TABLE, без комментариев сверху:

SQL

CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS users (
  id                INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
  primary_provider  TEXT NOT NULL,
  primary_uid       TEXT NOT NULL,
  handle            TEXT NOT NULL,
  avatar_url        TEXT,
  role              TEXT NOT NULL DEFAULT 'user',
  tos_accepted_at   INTEGER,
  tos_version       TEXT,
  github_login      TEXT,
  github_uid        TEXT,
  github_token_enc  TEXT,
  github_scope      TEXT,
  github_linked_at  INTEGER,
  created_at        INTEGER NOT NULL,
  banned_at         INTEGER,
  ban_reason        TEXT,
  UNIQUE(primary_provider, primary_uid)
);
→ Execute

Дальше по одному statement'у. Чтобы не возиться с копированием по кускам, вот все 13 команд готовыми блоками. Вставляй и выполняй каждый отдельно.

2.

SQL

CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_users_role ON users(role);

CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_users_github_uid ON users(github_uid);

CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS sessions (
  token       TEXT PRIMARY KEY,
  user_id     INTEGER NOT NULL,
  created_at  INTEGER NOT NULL,
  expires_at  INTEGER NOT NULL,
  FOREIGN KEY(user_id) REFERENCES users(id)
);

SQL

CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_sessions_user ON sessions(user_id);

SQL

CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS oauth_states (
  state        TEXT PRIMARY KEY,
  provider     TEXT NOT NULL,
  intent       TEXT NOT NULL,
  user_id      INTEGER,
  created_at   INTEGER NOT NULL,
  expires_at   INTEGER NOT NULL
);

SQL

CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_oauth_expires ON oauth_states(expires_at);

SQL

CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS items (
  id              TEXT PRIMARY KEY,
  kind            TEXT NOT NULL,
  name            TEXT NOT NULL,
  author_id       INTEGER NOT NULL,
  version         TEXT NOT NULL,
  summary         TEXT,
  tags            TEXT,
  language        TEXT,
  license         TEXT,
  nsfw            INTEGER NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
  size            INTEGER NOT NULL,
  gist_id         TEXT NOT NULL,
  gist_file       TEXT NOT NULL,
  gist_owner      TEXT NOT NULL,
  content_sha     TEXT,
  content_url     TEXT,
  preview_url     TEXT,
  status          TEXT NOT NULL DEFAULT 'live',
  status_reason   TEXT,
  install_count   INTEGER NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
  vote_score      INTEGER NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
  report_count    INTEGER NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
  created_at      INTEGER NOT NULL,
  updated_at      INTEGER NOT NULL,
  last_checked_at INTEGER,
  FOREIGN KEY(author_id) REFERENCES users(id)
);

SQL

CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS votes (
  user_id    INTEGER NOT NULL,
  item_id    TEXT NOT NULL,
  value      INTEGER NOT NULL,
  created_at INTEGER NOT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (user_id, item_id),
  FOREIGN KEY(user_id) REFERENCES users(id),
  FOREIGN KEY(item_id) REFERENCES items(id)
);
14.

SQL

CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS installs (
  user_id      INTEGER NOT NULL,
  item_id      TEXT NOT NULL,
  version      TEXT NOT NULL,
  installed_at INTEGER NOT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (user_id, item_id),
  FOREIGN KEY(user_id) REFERENCES users(id),
  FOREIGN KEY(item_id) REFERENCES items(id)
);
15.

SQL

CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS reports (
  id          INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
  user_id     INTEGER NOT NULL,
  item_id     TEXT NOT NULL,
  reason      TEXT NOT NULL,
  details     TEXT,
  status      TEXT NOT NULL DEFAULT 'open',
  created_at  INTEGER NOT NULL,
  resolved_at INTEGER,
  resolved_by INTEGER,
  FOREIGN KEY(user_id) REFERENCES users(id),
  FOREIGN KEY(item_id) REFERENCES items(id)
);
16.

SQL

CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_reports_status ON reports(status, created_at DESC);
Проверка
После всех 16 команд:

SQL

SELECT name FROM sqlite_master WHERE type='table';
Должно показать 7 таблиц:

users
sessions
oauth_states
items
votes
installs
reports
(плюс sqlite_sequence и _cf_KV — служебные, не считаем.)

Если выдаст всё это — schema залита, идёшь к Шагу 4 (создание Worker).
